***чад.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чадо.html>чад</a> (19982)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čadъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">smoke, fumes</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷēd-o-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чадо.html>чад</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čad</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чадо.html>ча́да</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>smoke, fumes</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> daze, frenzy</li></ol>

***чай.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>чай</a> (768)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">çay</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chinese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Chinese language">Chinese</a></span> <span class="Hani" lang="zh">茶</span> (<i><span class="tr Latn">chá</span></i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>чай</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čaj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>ча́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>чаи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>чаёв</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tea <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">drink</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">ани́совый<b><a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>чай</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">anísovyj<b>čaj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">anise <b>tea</b></span></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:китайский.html>кита́йский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>чай</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kitájskij <b>čaj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Chinese <b>tea</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цветочный.html>цвето́чный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>чай</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">cvetóčnyj <b>čaj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">rose <b>tea</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">цейло́нский <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>чай</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">cejlónskij <b>čaj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Ceylon <b>tea</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крепкий.html>кре́пкий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>чай</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krépkij <b>čaj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">strong <b>tea</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слабый.html>сла́бый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>чай</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">slábyj <b>čaj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">weak <b>tea</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сладкий.html>сла́дкий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>чай</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sládkij <b>čaj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">sweet <b>tea</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стакан.html>стака́н</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>ча́ю</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">stakán <b>čáju</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">a glass <b>of tea</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чашка.html>ча́шка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>ча́я</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čáška <b>čája</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">a cup <b>of tea</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пригласить.html>пригласи́ть</a> кого́-то <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чашка.html>ча́шку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>ча́я</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">priglasítʹ kovó-to na čášku čája</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to invite someone for <b>tea</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́йте</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:пожалуйста.html>пожа́луйста</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:кило.html>кило́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>ча́ю</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Dájte mne, požálujsta, kiló čáju.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I’d like a kilo of <b>tea</b>, please.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>ча́й</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dátʹ na <b>čáj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to leave a tip</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>tea plant <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content"><i>Camellia sinensis</i>, <i>Thea sinensis</i></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***чайка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чайка.html>ча́йка</a> (7722)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čajьka</i>, from onomatopoeia of cry *kē.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чайка.html>ча́йка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čájka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чайка.html>ча́йки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чайка.html>ча́йки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чаек.html>ча́ек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>seagull</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чайник.html>ча́йник</a> (3530)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>чай</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čaj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чайник.html>ча́йник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čájnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чайник.html>ча́йника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чайник.html>ча́йники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чайник.html>ча́йников</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>teapot, teakettle, kettle</li>
<li>dummy, novice, no-good</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чайный.html>ча́йный</a> (6053)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>чай</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čaj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чайный.html>ча́йный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čájnyj</span>) (<i>rare comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ча́йнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ча́йней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tea
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чайный.html>ча́йная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ложка.html>ло́жка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čájnaja</b> lóžka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">teaspoon</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чайный.html>ча́йный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лист.html>лист</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čájnyj</b> list</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tea leaf</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>tea-scented, tea-colored
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чайный.html>ча́йная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:роза.html>ро́за</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čájnaja</b> róza</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tea rose; tea-colored rose</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***чан.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чан.html>чан</a> (12900)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тшанъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tšanŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тчанъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tčanŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">дъщанъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dŭščanŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">made of boards</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, cognate to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доска.html>доска́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">doská</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дощатый.html>доща́тый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">doščátyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чан.html>чан</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čan</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чан.html>ча́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чан.html>чаны́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чан.html>ча́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чан.html>чано́в</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чан.html>ча́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tub, vat, tank; tun</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čara</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чара.html>ча́ра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čára</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чара.html>ча́ры</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чара.html>ча́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чара.html>ча́р</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чарка.html>ча́рка</a> (24809)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чара.html>ча́ра</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čára</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чарка.html>ча́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čárka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чарка.html>ча́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чарка.html>ча́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чарка.html>ча́рок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cup, glass, goblet <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">for drinking alcohol</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>cup <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">volume of liquid that can fit in such a vessel</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/charka" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:charka">charka</a>, a unit of liquid measure in Russia till 1925 containing 123 ml</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чародей.html>чароде́й</a> (5529)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">чародѣи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čaroděi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čarodějь</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čarъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sorcery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dějati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to do</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чародей.html>чароде́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čarodéj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чародей.html>чароде́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чародей.html>чароде́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чародей.html>чароде́ев</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чародейка.html>чароде́йка</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">чароде́йский</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sorcerer, magician, wizard

***час.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>час</a> (149)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">часъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">časŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*časъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>час</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čas</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>ча́са</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часа́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="deprecated-label">singular</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hour, o'clock, time, time of day
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>час</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kotóryj <b>čas</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What <b>time</b> is it?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́ром</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часу́</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V kotórom <b>časú</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">At what <b>time</b>?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>час</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čas</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>one o’clock</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>час</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>но́чи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čas</b> nóči</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one <b>a.m.</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>час</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>čas</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">at <b>one o’clock</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>час</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">odín <b>čas</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">one <b>hour</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часа́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dva <b>časá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">two <b>o’clock</b>; two <b>hours</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часа́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v dva <b>časá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">at two <b>o’clock</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="deprecated-label">plural</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hours, o'clock
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часо́в</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pjatʹ <b>časóv</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">five <b>o’clock</b>; five <b>hours</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="deprecated-label">plural</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> clock, watch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мои́х</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часа́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na moíx <b>časáx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">by my <b>watch</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:брат.html>бра́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несколько.html>не́сколько</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часо́в</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U mojevó bráta néskolʹko <b>časóv</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">My brother has several <b>watches</b>.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>иду́т</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éti <b>časý</b> ne idút.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This <b>clock/watch</b> doesn’t work.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> time, day
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>Час</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:расплата.html>распла́ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:настать.html>наста́л</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Čas</b> raspláty nastál.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The day of reckoning has arrived.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>After numbers ending with 2, 3 or 4 (except for those ending with 12, 13 or 14), the stress of the genitive singular moves to the last syllable: <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часа́</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>два́дцать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часа́</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>со́рок</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:четыре.html>четы́ре</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часа́</a></b>.</span>
</p>

***часовой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:часовой.html>часово́й</a> (8447)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>час</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čas</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (meaning "hour" <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>) or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">časý</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (meaning "clock, watch" <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:часовой.html>часово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">časovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hour
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:часовой.html>часово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пояс.html>по́яс</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>časovój</b> pójas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">time zone</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>hour</b> zone</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>by the hour</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> watch, clock
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:часовой.html>часово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мастер.html>ма́стер</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>časovój</b> máster</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>watch</b>maker</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:часовой.html>часово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">časovój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:часовой.html>часово́го</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:часовой.html>часовы́е</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:часовой.html>часовы́х</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:часовой.html>часова́я</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sentry, sentinel</li></ol>

***частить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:частить.html>части́ть</a> (28633)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:частый.html>ча́стый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">částyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:частить.html>части́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">častítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to do something rapidly/hurriedly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>части</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́</a> ясне́й</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne časti, govorí jasnéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">don't gabble/jabber, speak more distinctly</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to visit someone frequently, to see much of someone</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>часть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">častʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ца</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:частица.html>части́ца</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">častíca</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:частица.html>части́цы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:частица.html>части́цы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:частица.html>части́ц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fraction <i>(of)</i>, (little) part <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбиться.html>разби́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мелкий.html>ме́лкие</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:частица.html>части́цы</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">razbítʹsja na mélkije <b>častícy</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to break into smithereens [tiny pieces]</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> particle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заряжённый.html>заряжённая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:частица.html>части́ца</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zarjažónnaja <b>častíca</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">charged particle</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> particle</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:частично.html>части́чно</a> (6351)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
